msg:The overall feeling is very bad. After leaving Baotou, I chose Shangri-La in Hohhot. Without comparison, there is no harm. Regardless of the age of the hotel, room layout, hotel facilities or service procedures, the two hotels are almost exactly the same, but the service level, hotel The basic management of Shangri-La in Baotou is completely different. I suggest the management of Shangri-La in Baotou go to the Shangri-La in Hohhot to study hard. The following are negative reviews:

One is the service. The service process is not just for formality. I feel that there is poor communication among various parts of the hotel. The employees are confused and want to do a good job, but they are at a loss. There is a problem with the overall service. It is not the problem of individual employees. The management should go to Shangri-La Hohhot. Study and study.

The second is the hardware aspect. The two hotels are products of the same era, and the room facilities will have common flaws, but the hotel in Hohhot will continue to improve. To give a few examples, such as dim room lighting and few charging ports, the Shangri-La in Hohhot will Set a desk lamp on the desk, and add some lighting facilities and charging sockets in the room; for example, the original design of the bathroom door and toilet was very uncomfortable, so the Shangri-La in Hohhot changed it to a sliding door. Small changes can show the meticulousness of the management of Shangri-La Hohhot.

The worst experience of Sanbaotou Shangri-La comes from the countless smokers gathered from the elevator entrance in the basement parking lot to the elevator entrance in the lobby. They are blocked at the elevator entrance and filled with smoke. There are also people smoking in the lobby, but no one cares about it. There is a big no-smoking sign at the door. In vain...

The fourth reason for escaping from Shangri-La Baotou is that the eighth floor of the hotel is being renovated, but inferior decoration materials permeate the entire hotel, and the strong smell is carried from the elevator room to every floor. Can't we use better materials? It is harmful to the guests, and it has an even greater impact on the hotelâ€™s own staff!

One advantage is that the breakfast on the second floor of Shangri-La Hotel in Baotou is better than the breakfast on the second floor of Shangri-La in Hohhot in terms of variety, quality and taste. However, the VIP pavilion of Shangri-La in Hohhot is so good that it perfectly makes up for the shortcomings.

I also love Baotou, and I hope the hotel can improve and enhance Baotou instead of disappointing it.
